[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 1146002
     - Topic: Stress at work
     - Question number: 7
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Stress at work with 7 questions

-------------------
-------------------

Explanation: 

Here is the generated questionnaire on Stress at work with 7 questions:

{

    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "stress_at_work",

        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "q1",
            "NAME": "How often do you feel stressed at work?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Never"},
              {"ANSWER": "Rarely"},
              {"ANSWER": "Sometimes"},
              {"ANSWER": "Often"},
              {"ANSWER": "Almost always"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "q2",
            "NAME": "What are the main sources of stress in your work?",
            "TYPE_ID": 2,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Workload"},
              {"ANSWER": "Colleagues"},
              {"ANSWER": "Manager"},
              {"ANSWER": "Deadlines"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "q3",
            "NAME": "How do you typically handle stress at work?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "I take a break"},
              {"ANSWER": "I talk to a colleague"},
              {"ANSWER": "I try to focus on the task"},
              {"ANSWER": "I take some time off"},
              {"ANSWER": "I don't handle it well"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "q4",
            "NAME": "Do you feel that your workload is manageable?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Yes"},
              {"ANSWER": "No"},
              {"ANSWER": "Sometimes"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "q5",
            "NAME": "How would you rate your overall job satisfaction?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 5,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Very satisfied"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat satisfied"},
              {"ANSWER": "Neutral"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat dissatisfied"},
              {"ANSWER": "Very dissatisfied"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "q6",
            "NAME": "Have you experienced any physical symptoms due to stress at work?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 6,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Yes"},
              {"ANSWER": "No"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "q7",
            "NAME": "What changes would you like to see to reduce stress at work?",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 7,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "More flexible working hours"},
              {"ANSWER": "Clearer goals and expectations"},
              {"ANSWER": "More support from management"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```
This questionnaire is designed to assess the level of stress experienced by employees at work and to identify potential sources of stress. It also asks about the employee's coping mechanisms, job satisfaction, and physical symptoms related to stress. The final question encourages employees to suggest changes that could reduce stress at work.

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500000005
     - Topic: Course feedback
     - Question number: 5
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Course feedback with 5 questions

-------------------
-------------------

          {
            "CODE": "Q1",
            "NAME": "What did you like most about the course?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "The instructor's teaching style"},
              {"ANSWER": "The course material was relevant and engaging"},
              {"ANSWER": "The opportunity to work on projects"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q2",
            "NAME": "What did you find most challenging about the course?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "The pace of the course was too fast"},
              {"ANSWER": "The material was too difficult"},
              {"ANSWER": "I had trouble understanding the concepts"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q3",
            "NAME": "How would you rate the overall quality of the course?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "1 (very poor)"},
              {"ANSWER": "2"},
              {"ANSWER": "3"},
              {"ANSWER": "4"},
              {"ANSWER": "5 (excellent)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q4",

  }

This questionnaire contains 5 questions, each with a different type (ID: 1, 1, 3, 2, 1 respectively). The questions are designed to gather feedback on the course, including what was liked most, what was most challenging, the overall quality of the course, suggestions for improvement, and whether the course would be recommended to others.

     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100013
     - Topic: Employee Performance
     - Question number: 10
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User:

            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.

 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.

Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User:

     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

              {"ANSWER": "Poor"}
            ]

 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.

Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Quality of Diversity Training Programs with 7 questions

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
Explanation: Here is the generated questionnaire in JSON format:

```
{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "DIVERSITY_TRAINING",
        "NAME": "Quality of Diversity Training Programs",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,
        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "Q1",
            "NAME": "How would you rate the overall quality of the diversity training programs provided by your organization?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Excellent"},
              {"ANSWER": "Good"},
              {"ANSWER": "Fair"},
              {"ANSWER": "Poor"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q2",
            "NAME": "Do you feel that the diversity training programs have helped to increase your understanding of different cultures and perspectives?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Yes"},
              {"ANSWER": "No"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q3",
            "NAME": "Have you noticed any changes in your behavior or attitudes towards colleagues from diverse backgrounds after participating in the diversity training programs?",
            "TYPE_ID": 2,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Yes, significantly"},
              {"ANSWER": "Yes, slightly"},
              {"ANSWER": "No"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q4",
            "NAME": "How would you rate the effectiveness of the diversity training programs in addressing unconscious bias?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Excellent"},
              {"ANSWER": "Good"},
              {"ANSWER": "Fair"},
              {"ANSWER": "Poor"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q5",
            "NAME": "Do you think the diversity training programs have helped to create a more inclusive work environment?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 5,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Yes"},
              {"ANSWER": "No"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q6",
            "NAME": "What do you think is the most effective way to measure the success of diversity training programs?",
            "TYPE_ID": 6,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 6,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Feedback from participants"},
              {"ANSWER": "Changes in behavior or attitudes"},
              {"ANSWER": "Increased diversity in the workplace"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q7",
            "NAME": "Do you have any suggestions for improving the diversity training programs?",
            "TYPE_ID": 8,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 7,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Yes, [insert suggestion]"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

This questionnaire has 7 questions, with a mix of rating scales, multiple-choice, and open-ended questions. The questions are designed to assess the quality of diversity training programs and gather feedback from participants.

This questionnaire contains 6 questions that aim to gather feedback on the recognition and rewards system in your organization. The questions cover topics such as recognition, motivation, effectiveness, and suggestions for improvement. The question types used are ID (1), DESCRIPTION, which is suitable for questions that require a single answer from a list, and TYPE_ID (3), DESCRIPTION, which is suitable for questions that require a rating or a scale-based answer.

        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.

            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.

 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.

 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.

 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Training and Development Programs with 5 questions

{

    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "TDP_1",
        "NAME": "Training and Development Programs",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,
        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "Q1",
            "NAME": "What is the most important aspect of a training program for you?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Practical skills"},
              {"ANSWER": "Theoretical knowledge"},
              {"ANSWER": "Networking opportunities"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q2",
            "NAME": "How do you currently stay up-to-date with industry developments?",
            "TYPE_ID": 2,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Attending conferences and seminars"},
              {"ANSWER": "Reading industry publications"},
              {"ANSWER": "Participating in online forums and communities"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q3",
            "NAME": "What would you like to see changed or improved in our current training programs?",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "More hands-on training"},
              {"ANSWER": "More opportunities for feedback and discussion"},
              {"ANSWER": "More relevant and timely topics"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q4",
            "NAME": "How do you rate the effectiveness of our current training programs?",
            "TYPE_ID": 8,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Very effective"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat effective"},
              {"ANSWER": "Not very effective"},
              {"ANSWER": "Not at all effective"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q5",
            "NAME": "What would you like to see as a priority in our future training and development programs?",
            "TYPE_ID": 6,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 5,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Emphasis on leadership development"},
              {"ANSWER": "Emphasis on technical skills"},
              {"ANSWER": "Emphasis on soft skills"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

```
{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "TRAINING_DEV_PROGRAMS",
        "NAME": "Training and Development Programs",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,
        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "Q1",
            "NAME": "How would you rate the overall effectiveness of our current training and development programs?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "Very Effective"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Somewhat Effective"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Not Very Effective"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Not at All Effective"
              }
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q2",
            "NAME": "Which of the following training topics would you like to see more emphasis on in our future programs?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "Leadership Development"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Communication Skills"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Time Management"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"
              }
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q3",
            "NAME": "How often do you feel that you are able to apply the skills and knowledge learned in our training programs to your daily work?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "Almost Always"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Most of the Time"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Some of the Time"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Rarely"
              }
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q4",
            "NAME": "What do you think is the most significant barrier to your participation in our training and development programs?",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "Lack of Time"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Cost or Financial Constraints"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Location or Accessibility Issues"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"
              }
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q5",
            "NAME": "Would you be interested in participating in online or self-paced training programs?",
            "TYPE_ID": 2,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 5,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "Yes"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "No"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Maybe"
              }
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

This questionnaire has 5 questions, each with a different type:

* Q1 is a rating question, where the respondent can rate the effectiveness of our current training and development programs.
* Q2 is a multiple-choice question, where the respondent can choose one or more answers from a list.
* Q3 is a rating question, where the respondent can rate how often they apply the skills and knowledge learned in our training programs.
* Q4 is an open-ended question, where the respondent can provide feedback on what they think is the most significant barrier to their participation in our training and development programs.
* Q5 is a multiple-choice question, where the respondent can choose one or more answers from a list to indicate their interest in participating in online or self-paced training programs.

            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User:
